Active Hero's Echo
Master Level 1
Description [Master Level: 1]
Increases the Attack Power and Magic ATT of all nearby players.
Cooldown: 300 sec
Level 1 MP Cost: 30, Attack Power and Magic ATT: + 4%, Duration: 40 min


Active Elemental Slash
Master Level 1
Description Attack enemies in front of you with pure, primal energy.
Level 1 MP Cost: 0, Damage: 130%, Number of Attacks: 1, Max Enemies Hit: 3


Active Imperial Recall
Master Level 1
Description Return to the Empress using Shinsoo's power.
Level 1 MP Cost: 100, return to Ereve immediately.
Cooldown: 600 sec.


Passive Elemental Harmony
Master Level 1
Description Use the harmony of nature to build affinity for an element of your choosing.
Level 1 Dexterity increases 1 for every 2 levels the character gains


Passive Elemental Expert
Master Level 1
Description Become an expert of the elements to increase Attack Power and Magic ATT.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +10%


Passive Elemental Shift
Master Level 1
Description Jump in any direction except down by pressing a direction key and jump in midair.
Level 1 MP Cost: 4, jumps further in the appropriate direction

Passive Cygnus Blessing (Bowman)
Master Level 10
Description Blessings from an awakened Empress Cygnus protect you from harm.
This Link Skill can be stacked up to 5 times, once for each unique Cygnus Knights job character you have on this world.
Level 1 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +7, Abnormal Status Resistance: +1, All Elemental Resistance: +1%
10 Attack Power and Magic ATT: +25, Abnormal Status Resistance: +15, All Elemental Resistance: +15%

Active Wind Walk
Master Level 15
Description Your arrows walk on the wind, flying straight through any monsters they touch.
Level 1 MP Cost: 24, Moves along the platform on the ground and stops at the end of the platform. Can be used with Gust Swift in the air.
[Passive Effects: Speed: +21, Jump: +1, Max Speed: +6]

[Passive Effects: Speed: +35, Jump: +15, Max Speed: +20]

Active Trifling Wind I
Master Level 20
Description Summons the Spirit of Wind to confuse nearby enemies. Soul energy appears in the direction the Wind Archer is facing, except when using certain skills. Attacks by always including the boss with the highest Max HP within range.
Unaffected by attack reflection.
Can be toggled On/Off.
Level 20 required to learn Trifling Wind II.
Level 1 Max soul energy created: 1, Chance to create energy: 20%, Random enemies damaged: 132%, Chance to create enhanced soul energy: 3%, Damage of enhanced soul energy: 153%
20 Max soul energy created: 3, Chance to create energy: 30%, Random enemies damaged: 170%, Chance to create enhanced soul energy: 5%, Damage of enhanced soul energy: 210%

Active Erda Nova
Master Level 25
Description Collect Erda from within yourself and from the surrounding area, then detonate it around your enemies. The Erda of attacked enemies will become disrupted, which will bind their movements. Can deal damage to enemies even when they are under Attack Ignore. Also ignores Attack Reflection.
Level 1 HP Cost: 15% of Max HP, Damage: 156%, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Number of Attacks: 5, Bind Duration: 10 sec.
Bind Duration increases by up to 100% based on damage inflicted with Erda Nova.
Cooldown: 216 sec.

Active Erda Shower
Master Level 25
Description Fires a blast of compressed Erdas at nearby enemies.
Pressing the skill key with the down arrow key summons an Erda Fountain, an object filled with pure Erda.
With Action Customization enabled, you can summon Erda Fountain by pressing its skill key again, without the use of the arrow keys.
Right-click to toggle Action Customization ON/OFF
Level 1 HP Cost: 3000
Erdas Shower
Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 6, Cooldown reduced by 2 sec per attacked enemy
Cooldown: 40 sec
Erda Fountain
Object Summon Duration: 60 sec. Every time enemies in a map with the summoned object are defeated, the Erda released from the enemies condenses around the object.
Defeating 12 or more will release the gathered Erda, Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 465%, Number of Attacks: 4
Cooldown: 60 sec
Cooldown shared with Erdas Shower and Erda Fountain.

Active Decent Holy Fountain
Master Level 25
Description Summon a Holy Fountain that restores party members' HP. Even party members with the Undead status can use it. Approach the fountain and press the up arrow key to heal.
Can't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain or Decent Holy Fountain already exists.
If the Decent Holy Fountain disappears before its duration ends, a Vestige of Divinity will remain. cCan't be used on a map where another party member's Holy Fountain, Decent Holy Fountain, or Vestige of Divinity already exists.
Not affected by effects which reset cooldowns, increase recovery skill potency, or increase summon duration. Cannot be summoned near a portal.
Level 1 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 31 sec, restores 5% HP when used, able to use 5 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 89 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +1]
25 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 55 sec, restores 30% HP when used, able to use 17 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 65 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +5]
30 HP Cost: 5% of max HP, Duration: 60 sec, restores 35% HP when used, able to use 20 times total.
If it disappears before duration is up, Vestige of Divinity is created in the remaining time.
Cooldown: 60 sec
[Passive Effect - All Stats: +6]

Active Phalanx Charge
Master Level 25
Description Summons brave Spearmen of the Cygnus Knights to charge enemies in a phalanx formation. The spearmen slow down upon touching an enemy. Press the skill key again to change their direction of movement. Unaffected by attack reflection and can be resisted by some monsters.

Class-Specific Skills

Show/hide all levels
Active Howling Gale
Master Level 25
Description Summons a ferocious gust to punish your enemies.
Consumes 1 wind energy upon summoning. Using the skill with the down arrow key consumes 2 of your wind energy to summon a stronger gust. Using it with the up arrow key consumes 3 of your wind energy to summon 2 strong gusts.
The gust moves by continuously targeting the boss with the highest HP within the area, and reduces speed when attacking the enemy. There can only be 1 gust at a time, and it is unaffected by attack reflection.
Right-click to toggle speed reduction mode ON/OFF.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500, consumes wind energy to summon a gust for 10 sec
The power of the summoned gust varies based on the amount of wind energy
1 - Max Enemies Hit: 10, Damage: 338%, Number of Attacks: 3, Gust Summoned: 1
2 - Max Enemies Hit: 15, Damage: 816%, Number of Attacks: 3, Gust Summoned: 1
3 - Max Enemies Hit: 15, Gust Damage: 816%, Number of Attacks: 3, Gust Summoned: 1. Max Enemies Hit: 15, Gust Damage: 394%, Number of Attacks: 3, Gust Summoned: 1
Wind energy increases by 1 every 20 sec and you can hold up to 3.

Wind energy increases by 1 every 20 sec and you can hold up to 3.

Active Merciless Winds
Master Level 25
Description Call upon the Spirit of Wind to conjure deadly homing projectiles that track down your foes. The Spirit of Wind targets the boss with the highest HP first.
Unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 MP Cost: 500, Duration: 8 sec. Creates 10 enemy-seeking Spirit Arrows that deal 432% damage 5 times.
If more than one Spirit Arrow strikes the same enemy, the Final Damage of each additional arrow is reduced by 15%.
Enemies hit by Spirit Arrows take 520% damage time every 1 sec for 9 sec
Cooldown: 10 sec

Active Gale Barrier
Master Level 25
Description Activate a wind barrier around yourself that will defend you and decimate your enemies. Creates a whirlwind when you attack to deal additional damage.
Elemental is consumed upon defending against an attack and the wind barrier will disappear when it's completely consumed. The whirlwind is unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 MP Cost: 1000, Duration: 45 sec, creates a wind barrier with the 300 Elemental
Damage is nullified when the 1 Elemental is used for damage equal to 1% of max HP when hit. Also applies to attacks that deal damage proportional to the max HP.
Launches 3 whirlwinfloor(s) that deal(s) 572% damage every 2 sec upon attack. Decreases the Final Damage of the whirlwind by 50% if multiple whirlwinds attack 1 enemy.
Cooldown: 90 sec
25 MP Cost: 1000, Duration: 45 sec, creates a wind barrier with the 300 Elemental
Damage is nullified when the 1 Elemental is used for damage equal to 1% of max HP when hit. Also applies to attacks that deal damage proportional to the max HP.
Launches 3 whirlwinfloor(s) that deal(s) 1100% damage every 2 sec upon attack. Decreases the Final Damage of the whirlwind by 50% if multiple whirlwinds attack 1 enemy.
Cooldown: 90 sec
30 MP Cost: 1000, Duration: 45 sec, creates a wind barrier with the 300 Elemental
Damage is nullified when the 1 Elemental is used for damage equal to 1% of max HP when hit. Also applies to attacks that deal damage proportional to the max HP.
Launches 3 whirlwinfloor(s) that deal(s) 1210% damage every 2 sec upon attack. Decreases the Final Damage of the whirlwind by 50% if multiple whirlwinds attack 1 enemy.
Cooldown: 90 sec

Active Vortex Sphere
Master Level 25
Description Condense powerful winds into a sphere, then launch it in a slow, straight line. A gust occurs periodically with the Vortex Sphere at the center, pulling in surrounding enemies. Unaffected by attack reflection.
Level 1 MP Cost: 750. Creates a Vortex Sphere, which moves on a collision course with the enemy. The sphere periodically attacks up to 10 enemies, for 467% damage, 6 times.
Decreases Vortex Sphere's speed by 50% for 1 sec if a Boss Monster is attacked.
Collision occurs up to 20 times for each enemy.
Cooldown: 30 sec.

Description Summon a Cyclic Ring that endlessly creates and destroys Sol Erda. The cycling Erda Flow attacks nearby enemies.
When a new ring is summoned, the Erda Flow of each ring is reduced. Cyclic rings can be summoned in midair but can't be summoned too close to or too far from an existing ring.
Cyclic Rings are unaffected by attack reflection.

Active Mistral Spring
Master Level 30
Description A spring of wind bursts from the powerful emerald, drawing in any curious spirits that cross its path.
At regular intervals, the excited wind spirits ride the emerald's breeze to attack nearby enemies.
When there is a Wind Spring present, you can press the skill key re-summon it based on your current location.

Lv. 10: Ignore Defense +20%
Lv. 20: Boss Damage +20%
Lv. 30: Ignore Defense +30% and Boss Damage +30%
Level 1 MP Cost: 1200, invincible during casting
Create 13 Wind Blades that attack up to 15 enemies with 858% damage 10 times with the Spirit Arrows from the emerald.
After the attack ends, a wind spring creates Spirit Arrows to attack the enemy for 20 seconds
Replacement Cooldown: 3 sec
Spirit Arrows: create 13 Spirit Arrows that attack with 682% damage 5 times
Excited Spirit Arrows: create 5 Excited Spirit Arrows that attack with 744% damage 6 times
Strong Spirit Arrows: create 3 Strong Spirit Arrows that attack with 666% damage 7 times
Cooldown: 360 sec
30 MP Cost: 1200, invincible during casting
Create 13 Wind Blades that attack up to 15 enemies with 1670% damage 10 times with the Spirit Arrows from the emerald.
After the attack ends, a wind spring creates Spirit Arrows to attack the enemy for 20 seconds
Replacement Cooldown: 3 sec
Spirit Arrows: create 13 Spirit Arrows that attack with 1320% damage 5 times
Excited Spirit Arrows: create 5 Excited Spirit Arrows that attack with 1440% damage 6 times
Strong Spirit Arrows: create 3 Strong Spirit Arrows that attack with 1275% damage 7 times
Cooldown: 360 sec
